    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[ActualPoints], [s].[Code], [s].[CompilationErrors], [s].[ContestId], [s].[CreatedOn], [s].[DeletedOn], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[ModifiedOn], [s].[PracticeId], [s].[ProblemId], [s].[SubmisionDate], [s].[UserId]

    WHERE [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [s].[ProblemId] = @__problemId_0 AND [s].[UserId] = @__userId_1 AND ((
        SELECT COUNT(*)
        FROM [ExecutedTests] AS [e]
        WHERE [s].[Id] = [e].[SubmissionId]) > 0 OR ([s].[CompilationErrors] IS NOT NULL))
    ORDER BY [s].[SubmisionDate] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_2 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_3 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[AllowedMemoryInMegaBytes], [p].[AllowedMinCodeDifferenceInPercentage], [p].[AllowedTimeInMilliseconds], [p].[AutomatedTestingProject], [p].[CreatedOn], [p].[DeletedOn], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsExtraTask], [p].[LessonId], [p].[MaxPoints], [p].[ModifiedOn], [p].[Name], [p].[OrderBy], [p].[SubmissionType], [p].[TestingStrategy], [p].[TimeIntervalBetweenSubmissionInSeconds]
    FROM [Problems] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t0] ON [t].[ProblemId] = [t0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [ExecutedTests] AS [e0] ON [t].[Id] = [e0].[SubmissionId]
ORDER BY [t].[SubmisionDate] DESC, [t].[Id], [t0].[Id]

FROM (
    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[ActualPoints], [s].[Code], [s].[CompilationErrors], [s].[ContestId], [s].[CreatedOn], [s].[DeletedOn], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[ModifiedOn], [s].[PracticeId], [s].[ProblemId], [s].[SubmisionDate], [s].[UserId]
    FROM [Submissions] AS [s]
    WHERE [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [s].[ProblemId] = @__problemId_0 AND [s].[UserId] = @__userId_1 AND ((
        SELECT COUNT(*)
        FROM [ExecutedTests] AS [e]
        WHERE [s].[Id] = [e].[SubmissionId]) > 0 OR ([s].[CompilationErrors] IS NOT NULL))
    ORDER BY [s].[SubmisionDate] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_2 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_3 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[AllowedMemoryInMegaBytes], [p].[AllowedMinCodeDifferenceInPercentage], [p].[AllowedTimeInMilliseconds], [p].[AutomatedTestingProject], [p].[CreatedOn], [p].[DeletedOn], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsExtraTask], [p].[LessonId], [p].[MaxPoints], [p].[ModifiedOn], [p].[Name], [p].[OrderBy], [p].[SubmissionType], [p].[TestingStrategy], [p].[TimeIntervalBetweenSubmissionInSeconds]
    FROM [Problems] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t0] ON [t].[ProblemId] = [t0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [ExecutedTests] AS [e0] ON [t].[Id] = [e0].[SubmissionId]
ORDER BY [t].[SubmisionDate] DESC, [t].[Id], [t0].[Id]

FROM (
    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[ActualPoints], [s].[Code], [s].[CompilationErrors], [s].[ContestId], [s].[CreatedOn], [s].[DeletedOn], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[ModifiedOn], [s].[PracticeId], [s].[ProblemId], [s].[SubmisionDate], [s].[UserId]

    WHERE [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [s].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [s].[ProblemId] = @__problemId_0 AND [s].[UserId] = @__userId_1 AND ((
        SELECT COUNT(*)
        FROM [ExecutedTests] AS [e]
        WHERE [s].[Id] = [e].[SubmissionId]) > 0 OR ([s].[CompilationErrors] IS NOT NULL))
    ORDER BY [s].[SubmisionDate] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_2 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_3 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[AllowedMemoryInMegaBytes], [p].[AllowedMinCodeDifferenceInPercentage], [p].[AllowedTimeInMilliseconds], [p].[AutomatedTestingProject], [p].[CreatedOn], [p].[DeletedOn], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[IsExtraTask], [p].[LessonId], [p].[MaxPoints], [p].[ModifiedOn], [p].[Name], [p].[OrderBy], [p].[SubmissionType], [p].[TestingStrategy], [p].[TimeIntervalBetweenSubmissionInSeconds]
    FROM [Problems] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t0] ON [t].[ProblemId] = [t0].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [ExecutedTests] AS [e0] ON [t].[Id] = [e0].[SubmissionId]
ORDER BY [t].[SubmisionDate] DESC, [t].[Id], [t0].[Id]

    WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [t] ON [u].[ContestId] = [t].[Id]
